[2025-09-04 16:08:12 UTC] InverseEntropy_: when a star dies it ejects all of it's matter in a supernova, and the core either collapses into a dark vortex of gravity known as a black hole, or a white dwarf (our sun will become this). Sometimes, the matter in the core ejects all of the protons and electrons, resulting in a core made up of neutrons, thus resulting in a Neutron Star.
